      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/7084.Karl_Marx">About Karl Marx</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/7084.Karl_Marx"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1523865402p3/7084.jpg);'></div>
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__widgetContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>
<a href="/author/show/7084.Karl_Marx">Karl Marx
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__followerCount'>
3,309
followers
</div>

</div>
</div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer3333381218565417944"><b>Karl Marx,</b> Ph.D. (University of Jena, 1841) was a social scientist who was a key contributor to the development of Communist theory.<br/><br/>Descended from a long line of rabbis, Marx born in Prussian Rhineland. His father converted to Protestantism shortly before Karl's birth. Educated at the Universities of Bonn, Jena, and Berlin, Marx founded the Socialist newspaper Vorwarts in 1844 in Paris. After bein</span>
  <span id="freeText3333381218565417944" style="display:none"><b>Karl Marx,</b> Ph.D. (University of Jena, 1841) was a social scientist who was a key contributor to the development of Communist theory.<br /><br />Descended from a long line of rabbis, Marx born in Prussian Rhineland. His father converted to Protestantism shortly before Karl's birth. Educated at the Universities of Bonn, Jena, and Berlin, Marx founded the Socialist newspaper Vorwarts in 1844 in Paris. After being expelled from France at the urging of the Prussian government, which "banished" Marx in absentia, Marx studied economics in Brussels. He and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2900919.Engels" title="Engels" rel="nofollow noopener">Engels</a> founded the Communist League in 1847 and published the <i>Communist Manifesto</i>. After the failed revolution of 1848 in Germany, in which Marx participated, he eventually wound up in London. Marx worked as foreign correspondent for several U.S. publications. His <i>Das Kapital</i> came out in three volumes (1867, 1885 and 1894). Marx organized the International and helped found the Social Democratic Party of Germany. Although Marx was not religious, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/17854.Bertrand_Russell" title="Bertrand Russell" rel="nofollow noopener">Bertrand Russell</a> later remarked, "His belief that there is a cosmic force called Dialectical Materialism which governs human history independently of human volitions, is mere mythology" (Portraits from Memory, 1956). Marx once quipped, "All I know is that I am not a Marxist" (according to Engels in a letter to C. Schmidt; see <i>Who's Who in Hell</i> by Warren Allen Smith). D. 1883.<br /><br />Marx began co-operating with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/1149239.Bruno_Bauer" title="Bruno Bauer" rel="nofollow noopener">Bruno Bauer</a> on editing <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6188.Hegel" title="Hegel" rel="nofollow noopener">Hegel</a>'s Philosophy of Religion in 1840. Marx was also engaged in writing his doctoral thesis, The Difference Between the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2751823.Democritean" title="Democritean" rel="nofollow noopener">Democritean</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/114041.Epicurean" title="Epicurean" rel="nofollow noopener">Epicurean</a> Philosophy of Nature, which he completed in 1841. It was described as "a daring and original piece of work in which Marx set out to show that theology must yield to the superior wisdom of philosophy": the essay was controversial, particularly among the conservative professors at the University of Berlin. Marx decided, instead, to submit his thesis to the more liberal University of Jena, whose faculty awarded him his PhD in April 1841. As Marx and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/1149239.Bauer" title="Bauer" rel="nofollow noopener">Bauer</a> were both atheists, in March 1841 they began plans for a journal entitled <i>Archiv des Atheismus</i> (Atheistic Archives), but it never came to fruition.<br /><br />Marx has been described as one of the most influential figures in human history. Marx is typically cited, with Émile Durkheim and Max Weber, as one of the three principal architects of modern social science.<br /><br />More: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Karl_Marx">http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Karl_Marx</a><br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://plato.stanford.edu/entries/marx/">http://plato.stanford.edu/entries/marx/</a><br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.econlib.org/library/Enc/bios/Marx.html">http://www.econlib.org/library/Enc/bi...</a><br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.marxists.org/archive/marx/bio/marx/eng-1869.htm">http://www.marxists.org/archive/marx/...</a><br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.historyguide.org/intellect/marx.html">http://www.historyguide.org/intellect...</a><br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/history/historic_figures/marx_karl.shtml">http://www.bbc.co.uk/history/historic...</a><br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.spartacus.schoolnet.co.uk/TUmarx.htm">http://www.spartacus.schoolnet.co.uk/...</a><br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.britannica.com/EBchecked/topic/367265/Karl-Marx">http://www.britannica.com/EBchecked/t...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="3333381218565417944" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
</div>

      <div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/work/quotes/15400404-die-deutsche-ideologie">Quotes from The German Ideolo...</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;The ideas of the ruling class are in every epoch the ruling ideas, i.e. the class which is the ruling material force of society, is at the same time its ruling intellectual force. The class which has the means of material production at its disposal, has control at the same time over the means of mental production, so that thereby, generally speaking, the ideas of those who lack the means of mental production are subject to it. The ruling ideas are nothing more than the ideal expression of the dominant material relationships, the dominant material relationships grasped as ideas.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/352090-the-ideas-of-the-ruling-class-are-in-every-epoch">142 likes</a>
            </nobr>
            <div class="clear"></div>
          </div>
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;For as soon as the distribution of labour comes into being, each man has a particular, exclusive sphere of activity, which is forced upon him and from which he cannot escape. He is a hunter, a fisherman, a herdsman, or a critical critic, and must remain so if he does not want to lose his means of livelihood; while in communist society, where nobody has one exclusive sphere of activity but each can become accomplished in any branch he wishes, society regulates the general production and thus makes it possible for me to do one thing today and another tomorrow, to hunt in the morning, fish in the afternoon, rear cattle in the evening, criticise after dinner, just as I have a mind, without ever becoming hunter, fisherman, herdsman or critic.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/8116796-for-as-soon-as-the-distribution-of-labour-comes-into">61 likes</a>
            </nobr>
            <div class="clear"></div>
          </div>
        <a class="actionLink" style="float: right" href="/work/quotes/15400404-die-deutsche-ideologie">More quotes&hellip;</a>
